3b) ^cyFVudFJ

2) Medical endoscopes allow doctors to examine internal organs without invasive surgery. Coherent fibre bundles are used to transmit an image from inside the body to an eyepiece. Non-coherent fibre bundles are used to transmit light into the body for illumination. These fibres do not need to be arranged in order as they are only carrying light not an image. The frequencies used are between (400-700nm) as this is visible light, which is needed for illumination and imaging. Endoscopes can be used with forceps and scissors for tissue removal, cameras, suction and irrigation systems, and electrocautery tools. Laser light is used for precision cutting or removing of tissues, sealing blood vessels and destroying tumors or kidney stones. Some safety precautions is that goggles are worn, the power levels are controlled, and fire safety measures are taken as lasers can ignite things. ^iOGLF4zm

1) Optical fibre cables are widely used in communication systems like the internet. They are good for long distance communication. The role of internal reflection, is that it enables the light to travel through the cables, as the reflection stops it escaping whilst continuously reflecting within the core. This happens because the core has a higher refractive index than the cladding. The frequencies used are usually 850nm, 1300nm, and 1550nm. These have minimal absorption and scattering. Meaning they can travel long distances with low loss. Signal spreading happens and can lead to signals degrading over long distances. There are two types, modal dispersion and chromatic dispersion. Transmission times depend on the speed of light, light travels at around 200,000km/s in glass fibres. Typical data transmission speeds in fibre-optic cables ranges from 1Gb/s to 400Gb/s and more.   ^LJr3vjAG
